 clark hairaan the ki jis gend ko dephend karne ke liye unhone balla or pad ek saath aage badhaayaa tha, vah achaanak wicket main kaise ghus gai
 However, Jadeja gave India a great success with a very good ball
 clark ne 31 gendon kaa saamana karte hue ek chakka lagaaya
 After this, as if Kovan also lost his morale and he lost his restraint on the total of 111 runs
 vah jadeja kii ek gend par balla laga baithe, jo wicket se sate captain dhoni ke gloves se takaraakar pehle slip main khadey virendra sahvaag ke paas gai, jinhone use lapakane main koi galati nahin kii
 Cowan scored 44 runs
 unhone 150 gedon kaa saamana karte hue chah chauke lagaae
 The team had high hopes from Moises Henriques, who replaced Kovan but after facing four balls, he was run out by Jadeja in an attempt to steal a run
 jadeja ne sidhe thro par henrics ko pavilion kii raah dikhaai
 The comments iske baad aswin ne apana pehla test khel rahe glen maxwell (8), mathew vade (10) or james patinson (0) tathaa jadeja ne peter sidle (4) ko out karte hue mehmaan team kii pari samet di
 Indian spinners took a total of 14 wickets in this match, with 20 wickets in Chennai
 australia ne match ke pehle din nau wicket par 237 ran banane ke baad apni pehali pari ghoshit kar di thi
 After this, India scored 503 runs in their first innings with the help of Cheteshwar Pujara (204) and Murali Vijay (167)
 bharat ko pehali pari ke aadhaar par 266 ranon kii badhat mili thi
 Saurashtra batsman Cheteshwar Pujara, who played a brilliant innings of 204 runs for India, was adjudged Man of the Match
 yah match bhartiya captain mahendra singh dhoni ke liye yaadgaar rahaa, kyonki isamen team ko jeet dilaane ke saath vah bharat ke sabase safal test captain ban gaye hai
 Dhoni overtook former captain Sourav Ganguly with 22 Test wins under whose leadership India won 21 Tests
 baharhaal, jaisaa ki ummid thi bhartiya gendaabaajon ne spin le rahi wicket par apni team ko mangalvaar ko match ke chauthe din pari kii jeet dilaane kii muhim shuru kii
 In this campaign, he had an unforeseen success and the team, trailing by 266 on the basis of first innings and 192 runs by the end of the third day, collapsed for 131 runs in their second innings just before lunch on the fourth day
 is match main bhartiya varchasv kaa alam yah rahaa ki puri australian team ne match main 368 ran batore, jaaki bharat ke do ballobaajon-pujaara (204) or murali vijay (167) ne duusare wicket ke liye 370 ran jode the
 Now both teams will turn to Mohali, where the third Test match will be played at Punjab Cricket Association Ground (PCA) from 18 February
 chauthe din australia ke liye din kii shuruyaat aid kowan or shen watson ne kii
 Cowan was unbeaten on 26 and Watson on nine runs
 tisare din mehmaan team ne david warner (26) philip huge (0) ke wicket ganvaakar 74 ran banaae the
 The day started badly for Australia
 watson apane tisare din ke score main bina koi ran jode ishanth sharma kii baahar jaati gend ke saath chhedhkhani ke prayaas main wicket ke peeche captain mahendra singh dhoni ke haathon lapke gaye
 After this, Cowan and captain Michael Clarke took care of and raised the score to 100
 aisa lag rahaa tha ki yah jodi australia ko mushkil se ubaarane kii ore agrasar ho sakati he, lekin 108 ranon ke kul yoga par rabindra jadeja ne ek behtareen gend par clark ko bold kar diya
 Clarke was surprised as to how the ball he had pushed forward to bat and padded suddenly turned into a wicket
 jo bhi ho lekin jadeja ne ek behad umdaa gend par bharat ko badi safalataa dilaai
 Clarke faced 31 balls and hit a six
 iske baad maano kowan kaa bhi manobal tut gaya or 111 ranon ke kul yoga par vah bhi apana sanyam kho bethe
 He sat on a ball from Jadeja, who collided with the glove of wicket-laden captain Dhoni and went to Virender Sehwag standing at first slip, who made no mistake in catching him
 kowan ne 44 ran banaae
 He hit six fours, facing 150 balls
 kowan kaa sthaan lene aae moysis henrics se team ko kaaphi ummiden thim lekin chaar gendon kaa saamana karne ke baad vah ek ran churaane ke prayaas main jadeja ke haathon ran out kar die gaye
 Jadeja showed Henriques the pavilion on a straight throw
 tippaniyan After this, Ashwin made his first Test playing Glenn Maxwell (8), Matthew Wade (10) and James Pattinson (0) and Jadeja dismissed Peter Siddle (4)

 iske baad bharat ne cheteshwar pujaara (204) or murali vijay (167) kii behtareen pariyon kii madad se apni pehali pari main 503 ran banaae the
 India had a lead of 266 runs on the basis of first innings
 yahaan ke ek jyotishi or saamaajik kaaryakarta ne jal sangrakshan ke liye jo kaam kiya he vah puure desh ke liye udhaaharan ban saktaa he
 The unique work of conserving water to be offered to the idols in temples is being done here
 apane chaheton ke bich guruji ke naam se prasiddh pandit purushottam goud ne pichley 13 varsho main rajasthan ke kareeb 300 mandiron main jalsangrakshan dhaanche kaa vikaas kiya he
 Gaud has been awarded several honors including Maharana Mewar Award for his remarkable work in the field of social service and astrology
 hindu mandiron main bhakton dwaara arpit lakhon galen jal naaliyon main bah jaataa tha
 Gaud said that in the year 2000, he started his Jalabhishek campaign
 41 varshiya jyotishi goud ne bataaya, "maine gaur kiya ki mandiron main shraddhaluon dwaara arpit jal puri tarah naaliyon main bekaar chalaa jaataa he
 So i thought of using them to recharge ground water
 " After this, he started collecting water in temples, especially pagoda
 bhoomi main bhejne se pehle jal ko kai filter chambaron se guzaara jaataa he
 Gaur said that under this project many tanks and borewells were built in the temples with public support
 goud ne kaha, "kuch mandiron main 30 foot gaharaa gaddha khodne kii jarurat padi taaki pratimaaon kaa jal sidhaa vahaan ekatrit ho sake
 a separate five-foot pit was needed to deposit the milk to be mounted on the statues
 " Gaur continued, "I was very happy when many scientists and groundwater experts came to my aid and put forward an organization called 'shiksha Samiti' in this work
 is santhaan ne hisaab lagaaya ki shahar main 300 se zyada mandir hai jahaan shravan maheene main rojaanaa kam se kam chaar karod 50 lakh litre jal bhagwaan shiv va anya devi devataaon kii pratimaaon par arpit kiya jaataa he
 "he said that apart from this waste, water and milk offered by the devotees also have an adverse effect on the environment
 tippaniyan Gaur said, "generally water and milk are allowed to flow freely near the temple
 isse aswasthkar vaataavaran paidaa hota he
 Mosquitoes and flies thrive around the temple
 " Regarding the difficulties faced in water conservation work, Gaud said that initially it was not easy to convince the priests
 unhone kaha ki unke prayaas ko kai pujaariyon ne andeh kii drushti se dekha
 Even when his supporters started collecting money for this project, the priests continued to ignore
 lekin aaj 300 mandir is abhiyaan se jude hai
 Pandit Purushottam Gaur, popularly known as Guruji among his favorites, has developed water conservation structures in nearly 300 temples in Rajasthan in the last 13 years
 samaaj seva or jyotish ke kshetra main ullekhneey kaam karne ke liye goud ko maharana mewar award samet kai sammaanon se nawaja ja chukaa he
 In Hindu temples, millions of gallons of water offered by devotees flowed into the drains
 goud ne bataaya ki varsh 2000 main unhone apana jalabhishek abhiyaan shuru kiya
 41-year-old astrologer Gaud said, "I noticed that the water offered by the devotees in the temples goes completely waste in the drains
 isliye mujhe inkaa bhoojal ko richarge karne main istemaal karne kii yukti suujhi
 " iske baad unhone mandiron khaas kar shivalayon main jal sangrah karne kaa kaam shuru kiya
 The water is passed through several filter chambers before being sent to land
 goud ne kaha ki is pariyojna ke tahat mandiron main jan sahyog se kai tanks or borwell kaa nirmaan karaayaa gaya
 Gaud said, "in some temples, a 30-foot deep pit was required to be dug so that the water of the idols could be collected directly there
 pratimaaon par chadhaae jane vaale doodh ko jamaa karne ke liye paanch foot ke gadde kii alag se jarurat padi
 " goud ne aage kaha, "mujhe tab behad khushi hui jab kai vaigyanik or bhoojal visheshgy meri madad ke liye saamne aae or 'shiksha samiti' naam ke ek sanghathan ko is kaam main aage kiya
 The institute calculated that there are more than 300 temples in the city where at least 40 million liters of water is offered daily in the month of Shravan to the idols of Lord Shiva and other deities
 " unhone kaha ki is barbaadi ke alaava shraddhaluon dwaara arpit jal or dugdh kaa paryaavaran par bhi vipareet prabhaav padataa he
 The comments goud ne bataaya, "aam taur par mandir ke sameep jal or dugdh ko nirbaadh bahane diya jaataa he
 This creates an unhealthy environment
 mandir ke chaaron ore machhar or mackhiyon ke palane kaa vaataavaran taiyaar ho jaataa he
 " jal sangrakshan ke kaam main pesh ai kathinaaiyon ke bare main goud ne bataaya ki shuru main iske liye pujaariyon ko manaa paanaa aasaan nahin tha
 He said that his efforts were viewed with suspicion by many priests
 yahaan tak ki jab unke samarthakon ne is pariyojna ke liye dhan jamaa karnaa shuru kiya tab bhi pujari anakani karte rahe
 But today 300 temples are associated with this campaign
 samaaj seva or jyotish ke kshetra main ullekhneey kaam karne ke liye goud ko maharana mewar award samet kai sammaanon se nawaja ja chukaa he
 In Hindu temples, millions of gallons of water offered by devotees flowed into the drains
 goud ne bataaya ki varsh 2000 main unhone apana jalabhishek abhiyaan shuru kiya
 41-year-old astrologer Gaud said, "I noticed that the water offered by the devotees in the temples goes completely waste in the drains
 isliye mujhe inkaa bhoojal ko richarge karne main istemaal karne kii yukti suujhi
 " iske baad unhone mandiron khaas kar shivalayon main jal sangrah karne kaa kaam shuru kiya
 The water is passed through several filter chambers before being sent to land
 goud ne kaha ki is pariyojna ke tahat mandiron main jan sahyog se kai tanks or borwell kaa nirmaan karaayaa gaya
 Gaud said, "in some temples, a 30-foot deep pit was required to be dug so that the water of the idols could be collected directly there
 pratimaaon par chadhaae jane vaale doodh ko jamaa karne ke liye paanch foot ke gadde kii alag se jarurat padi
 " goud ne aage kaha, "mujhe tab behad khushi hui jab kai vaigyanik or bhoojal visheshgy meri madad ke liye saamne aae or 'shiksha samiti' naam ke ek sanghathan ko is kaam main aage kiya
 The institute calculated that there are more than 300 temples in the city where at least 40 million liters of water is offered daily in the month of Shravan to the idols of Lord Shiva and other deities
 " unhone kaha ki is barbaadi ke alaava shraddhaluon dwaara arpit jal or dugdh kaa paryaavaran par bhi vipareet prabhaav padataa he
 The comments goud ne bataaya, "aam taur par mandir ke sameep jal or dugdh ko nirbaadh bahane diya jaataa he
 This creates an unhealthy environment
 mandir ke chaaron ore machhar or mackhiyon ke palane kaa vaataavaran taiyaar ho jaataa he
 " jal sangrakshan ke kaam main pesh ai kathinaaiyon ke bare main goud ne bataaya ki shuru main iske liye pujaariyon ko manaa paanaa aasaan nahin tha
 He said that his efforts were viewed with suspicion by many priests
 yahaan tak ki jab unke samarthakon ne is pariyojna ke liye dhan jamaa karnaa shuru kiya tab bhi pujari anakani karte rahe
 But today 300 temples are associated with this campaign
 hindu mandiron main bhakton dwaara arpit lakhon galen jal naaliyon main bah jaataa tha
 Gaud said that in the year 2000, he started his Jalabhishek campaign
 41 varshiya jyotishi goud ne bataaya, "maine gaur kiya ki mandiron main shraddhaluon dwaara arpit jal puri tarah naaliyon main bekaar chalaa jaataa he
 So i thought of using them to recharge ground water
 " After this, he started collecting water in temples, especially pagoda
 bhoomi main bhejne se pehle jal ko kai filter chambaron se guzaara jaataa he
 Gaur said that under this project many tanks and borewells were built in the temples with public support
 goud ne kaha, "kuch mandiron main 30 foot gaharaa gaddha khodne kii jarurat padi taaki pratimaaon kaa jal sidhaa vahaan ekatrit ho sake
 a separate five-foot pit was needed to deposit the milk to be mounted on the statues
 " Gaur continued, "I was very happy when many scientists and groundwater experts came to my aid and put forward an organization called 'shiksha Samiti' in this work
 is santhaan ne hisaab lagaaya ki shahar main 300 se zyada mandir hai jahaan shravan maheene main rojaanaa kam se kam chaar karod 50 lakh litre jal bhagwaan shiv va anya devi devataaon kii pratimaaon par arpit kiya jaataa he
 "he said that apart from this waste, water and milk offered by the devotees also have an adverse effect on the environment
 tippaniyan Gaur said, "generally water and milk are allowed to flow freely near the temple
 isse aswasthkar vaataavaran paidaa hota he
 Mosquitoes and flies thrive around the temple
 " Regarding the difficulties faced in water conservation work, Gaud said that initially it was not easy to convince the priests

 The UPA government, which has been criticizing the issue of two Italian marines not returning to India, has taken a strong stand
 pradhanmantri manmohan sinhane buudhvaar ko chetavanee di ki agar italy ne bhartiya machuaaron kii hatya karne vaale apane do marinon (nausainikon) ko bharat waapas bhejne ke apane aashwaasan ko puraa nahin kiya to iske parinaam bhugatne honge
 On the issue being raised by members after the Question Hour in the Lok Sabha, Singh said, 'there can be no two opinions that what the Italian government has done is not fair
 hamaari sarkaar pehle hi spasht kar chuki he ki italy kaa yah vyavhaar sweekaarya nahin he
 He has violated the assurance given to the Supreme Court
 unhone kaha ki in marinon ko bharat waapas bheje jane ke sandarbh main supreme court ko italy dwaara diye gayi aashwaasan kaa jis tarah ulanghan kiya gaya he, vah dwipaksheeya rishton ke hit main nahin he
 Singh said, "we have told the Government of Italy to honor the affidavit given in the Supreme Court and send it back to both the marines
" yadi waapas nahin bheja jaataa he to iske parinaam bhugatne honge
 'it is noteworthy that these two Italian marines had allegedly shot and killed two Indian fishermen in the Indian sea area after which they were arrested
 isse pehle in do marine ko christmas or nav varsh manaane apane desh jane kii anumati adaalat ne di thi
 An affidavit was given from Italy that both marines would return to India and they also returned
 lekin italy main chunaav ke dauraan matdaan ke liye inhen phir apane desh jane kii ijaajat di gayi thi

 shoonyakaal main bijepi ke varisht netaa jaswant singh ne yah maamla uthaate hue kaha ki italy ke in do marine ne antarrashtriya samudri kshetra main nahin balki bhartiya samudri kshetra main or hamaare tat ke nikat desh ke do machuaaron kii goli markar hatya kar di or baad main kaha ki unhone in machuaaron ko samudri dasyu samajhakar maaraa tha

 He questioned the government whether inmates in Indian jails are released from jail to celebrate Holi, Diwali or Eid or are allowed to go to the polls at the time of elections? If this is not the case, then why were Italian marines treated with such special treatment? Singh said that the apex court, on the assurance of the Italian ambassador, allowed these marines to go to their country, but there was a provision that they would remain in the custody of the police even while in Italy

 Earlier on Monday, the health of Shiv Sena MP Sanjay Raut had worsened
 unhen mumbai ke leelavati hospital main bhartee karaayaa gaya
 Sanjay Raut has been a great attacker on the BJP since the Maharashtra Assembly election results
 vah shivasena ke mukhpatr saamana ke kaaryakari sampadak bhi hai
 Sanjay Raut's health deteriorated at a time when Governor Bhagat Singh Koshyari invited Shiv Sena to form the government
 sanjay raut ke bhai sunil raut kaa kahana he ki pichley 15 din se unke seene main dard ho rahaa tha
 His checkup was also done
 haalanki chintaa kii koi baat nahin he
 He will be discharged from the hospital in a day or two
 notebandi ke virodh main or atm se paise nikaalane me logon ko lekar aa rahi pareshaani ko lekar lagaayi gai do yachikaaon par dilli hoicourt ne aaj sunwaayee ke dauraan kaha ki supreme court me pehle hi ye maamla lambit he or ham kuch vakt intjaar karnaa chaahate he
 The central government said that our transfer application is in the Supreme Court, the High Court has now given the date of December 8 for hearing
 sunwaayee ke dauraanyachikakartane kaha ki sarkaar ne bainko ko ye sunishchit karne ko kaha he ki ATM khule rahe or log paise nikaal sake, lekin bainko ne ATM ko taala laga rakhaa he
 Under Section 24 (2) of the RBI Act in the petition, the government has issued a notification to issue new notes, which is unconstitutional
 is dhara ke tahat sirf sarkaar notebandi kaa faisla le sakati he, nae note jari karne kaa nahin
 Issuance of 2000 Note It is mandatory for the government to issue notification under Section 24 (1) of RBI Act for issuing a new note
 yachika main kaha gaya he ki sarkaar kaa do hajaar ke note ko jari karnaa asanvaidhanik he, kyonki ye sidhe taur par arabiai act kaa ulanghan he
 The petition has also demanded that if the government itself is taking 500 and 1000 notes at places like petrol pumps, central stores, then the government itself is accepting black money from the people themselves
 agar sarkaar 8 november kii ghoshnaa ke baad jab khud ye note le sakati he to phir ise baaki jagahon par bhi (privet sector) chalaane kii ijaajat sarkaar ko aam logon kii deni chahie
 Food inflation declined for the second week in a row
 guuruuvaar ko jari aadhikarik aankadon ke mutabik isamen subjiyon or khaskar pyaaj kii keemton main tikhi giravat ne mahatvapurn bhoomika nibhaai
 Food inflation in the week ended 31 December -2
 9 fisadi rahi
 Last week it -3
 36 fisadi thi, jo april 2006 ke baad khaadya mahangaai dar kaa nichalaa str he
 Union Finance Minister Pranab Mukherjee said that prices will continue to fall in the coming months
 saptahik aankadon par pratikriya dete hue mukherjee ne kaha, "mahangaai main kami agle maheenon main jari rahegi
 During this period, the prices of manufactured goods will also fall and the prices of non-food items will also fall sharply
 " The minister said that by March this year, the inflation rate will come down to six to seven percent
 taaja aankadon ke mutabik navambar maah kii vaarshik mahangaai dar 9
 11 percent
 khaadya mahangaai dar lagbhag chah saal main pehali baar 24 disambar 2011 ko samaapt saptaah main nakaaratmak ankon main darj kii gai
 This brought relief to both the common man and policy makers
 taaja nakaaratmak dar main pichley saptaah kii oonchi dar or mausami aapurti ne mahatvapurn yogadan kiya
 Inflation was around 20 percent in the same period last year
 kendriya vaanijya or udyog mantralay dwaara jari aankadon ke mutabik subjiyon kii keemat pichley saal ke mukaable lagbhag aadhi dekhi gai
 20 in annual inflation rate
 12 fisadi yogadan karne vaale praathmik vastuon ke suchakank main aalochay avadhi main 0
 51 percent inflation was recorded
 isi avadhi main eendhan or bijli main 14
 45 percent inflation was recorded, up from 14 last week
 6 fisadi thi
 According to economists, due to the recent fall in food inflation and the reduction in annual inflation pressures, the Reserve Bank of India may consider cutting the key rates and the food inflation is likely to remain around zero till March
 khaadya suchakank ke tahat aane vaali kuch pramukh vastuon ke mulyon main pichley ek saal main aayaa utaar chadhaav is prakaar he : Onion: (-) 74
 77 fisadi Vegetable: (-) 49
 03 fisadi Fruit: 9 percent aalu : (-) 31

 22 percent anaaj : 2
 03 percent chaaval : 1
 7 percent comments gehun : (-) 3
 35 percent daal : 14
 72 percent khaadya mahangaai dar 31 disambar ko samaapt saptaah main -2
 It was 9 percent
 pichley saptaah yah -3
 36 percent, which is the lowest level of food inflation since April 2006
 kendriya vitt mantri pranab mukherjee ne kaha ki aane vaale maheenon main keemton main giravat jari rahegi
 Reacting to the weekly data, Mukherjee said, "the decrease in inflation will continue in the following months
 is dauraan vinirmit vastuon kii keemten bhi ghatengi or gaiyr-khaadya vastuon kii keemton main bhi teji se giravat hogi
 " mantri ne kaha ki is saal march tak mahangaai dar ghatakar chah se saat fisadi ho jaaegi
 According to the latest data, the annual inflation rate for the month of November is 9
 11 fisadi he
 Food inflation was recorded for the first time in nearly six years in negative numbers in the week ended 24 December 2011
 isse aam aadmi or niti nirmaataaon donon ko raahat mili
 Last week's high rate and seasonal supply contributed significantly to the fresh negative rate
 pichley saal kii samaan avadhi main mahangaai dar 20 fisadi ke aasapaas thi
 According to the data released by the Union Ministry of Commerce and Industry, the price of vegetables was seen at almost half of the previous year
 vaarshik mahangaai dar main 20
 0 in the primary articles index contributing 12 percent in the period under review
 51 fisadi mahangaai darj kii gai
 14 in fuel and electricity over the same period
 45 fisadi mahangaai darj kii gai, jo pichley saptaah 14
 Was 6 percent
 arthshaastriyon ke mutabik khaadya mahangaai dar main taaja giravat or vaarshik mahangaai dar ke dabaav main ai kami ke kaaran bhartiya rigerv bank mukhya daron main katautee karne par vichaar kar saktaa he or khaadya mahangaai dar march tak shunya ke aasapaas bani rahane kii sambhaavna he
